\"source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h\", \"symbol\": \"ListenSocketFactoryImpl::getListenSocket\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy listener manager lifecycle architecture is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the envoyproxy/envoy repository. The core components include:\\n\\n**Listener Manager Interface and Implementation**:\\n- `envoy/server/listener_manager.h` defines the `ListenerManager` interface with methods for listener lifecycle management: `addOrUpdateListener()`, `removeListener()`, `startWorkers()`, `stopWorkers()`, and `stopListeners()`.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h` and `.cc` provide the main implementation (`ListenerManagerImpl`) which manages listener addition/removal, coordinates with workers, and maintains three listener states: active, warming, and draining. The `DrainingFilterChainsManager` handles filter chain draining during listener updates.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h` and `.cc` implement the `ListenerImpl` class representing individual listeners. It includes `ListenSocketFactoryImpl` for socket creation and management, supporting both socket reuse_port and no-reuse_port modes for worker socket sharing.\\n\\n**Connection Handler and Worker Thread Assignment**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/connection_handler_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `ConnectionHandlerImpl` which manages the per-handler listener instances and assigns listeners to worker threads. It tracks active listeners by tag and address for TCP, UDP, QUIC, and internal listeners.\\n- `source/server/worker_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `WorkerImpl` which runs in a dedicated worker thread and coordinates with the main `ConnectionHandler` via its `handler_` member, which is a `ConnectionHandlerImpl`.\\n- `source/server/listener_manager_factory.h` defines factory interfaces for creating listener managers and connection handlers.\\n\\n**Active Listeners and Socket Sharing**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_listener.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveTcpListener` which wraps active TCP listeners and manages TCP connections. Multiple workers share sockets when bind_type is `NoReusePort`, with each worker getting the same socket from `ListenSocketFactoryImpl::getListenSocket(worker_index)`.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_socket.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveTcpSocket` which wraps accepted sockets going through listener filters.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_stream_listener_base.h` and `.cc` provide the base `ActiveStreamListenerBase` class and `OwnedActiveStreamListenerBase` mixin which owns active connections organized by filter chain in `ActiveConnections` containers.\\n- `source/server/active_listener_base.h` defines `ActiveListenerImplBase` base class for all active listeners with stats tracking.\\n- `source/server/active_udp_listener.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveUdpListenerBase` and `ActiveRawUdpListener` for UDP listeners.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_raw_udp_listener_config.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveRawUdpListenerFactory`.\\n\\n**Drain Mechanism**:\\n- `source/server/drain_manager_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `DrainManagerImpl` which manages the listener drain sequence, controlling when connections should be drained during shutdown.\\n- The listener manager's `drainListener()` method transitions listeners from active to draining state and schedules drain completion via `DrainingFilterChainsManager::startDrainSequence()`.\\n- Filter chains can be selectively drained via `inPlaceFilterChainUpdate()` which calls `drainFilterChains()` for updated listeners.\\n\\n**Filter Chain Management**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `FilterChainManagerImpl` and `FilterChainImpl` for managing filter chains per listener.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_factory_context_callback.h` defines the `FilterChainFactoryContextCreator` interface.\\n\\n**Dynamic Listener Configuration**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/lds_api.h` and `.cc` implement `LdsApiImpl` which subscribes to LDS updates from the control plane.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h` implements `ProdListenerComponentFactory` which creates sockets via `ListenerComponentFactory::createListenSocket()` with bind_type parameter controlling socket sharing strategy.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure**:\\n- `source/server/listener_hooks.h` defines `ListenerHooks` interface for integration testing during listener lifecycle events.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_info_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `ListenerInfoImpl` for listener metadata.\\n- `source/common/quic/active_quic_listener.h` and `.cc` implement QUIC-specific listener handling.\\n- `source/extensions/bootstrap/internal_listener/` provides internal listener registry and management.\\n- `source/extensions/listener_managers/validation_listener_manager/` provides a validation listener manager factory for config validation.\\n- `source/common/network/listen_socket_impl.h` and `.cc` implement socket binding and option handling.\\n\\nThe architecture uses a thread-per-worker design where the listener manager on the main thread coordinates listener lifecycle changes across worker threads via the connection handler. Socket sharing between workers is implemented through socket duplication for no-reuse_port mode (managed by `ListenSocketFactoryImpl`) or per-worker socket creation for reuse_port mode. Drain state transitions are coordinated through the drain manager and tracked via listener states (active, warming, draining).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":194,"cache_read_input_tokens":75811,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":194},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"325c41fa-f10f-41b1-bdf7-9e2f073c8966","uuid":"05d7781c-aa8a-4a65-b784-120b537a66b0"}

\"source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h\", \"symbol\": \"ListenSocketFactoryImpl::getListenSocket\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy listener manager lifecycle architecture is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the envoyproxy/envoy repository. The core components include:\\n\\n**Listener Manager Interface and Implementation**:\\n- `envoy/server/listener_manager.h` defines the `ListenerManager` interface with methods for listener lifecycle management: `addOrUpdateListener()`, `removeListener()`, `startWorkers()`, `stopWorkers()`, and `stopListeners()`.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h` and `.cc` provide the main implementation (`ListenerManagerImpl`) which manages listener addition/removal, coordinates with workers, and maintains three listener states: active, warming, and draining. The `DrainingFilterChainsManager` handles filter chain draining during listener updates.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h` and `.cc` implement the `ListenerImpl` class representing individual listeners. It includes `ListenSocketFactoryImpl` for socket creation and management, supporting both socket reuse_port and no-reuse_port modes for worker socket sharing.\\n\\n**Connection Handler and Worker Thread Assignment**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/connection_handler_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `ConnectionHandlerImpl` which manages the per-handler listener instances and assigns listeners to worker threads. It tracks active listeners by tag and address for TCP, UDP, QUIC, and internal listeners.\\n- `source/server/worker_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `WorkerImpl` which runs in a dedicated worker thread and coordinates with the main `ConnectionHandler` via its `handler_` member, which is a `ConnectionHandlerImpl`.\\n- `source/server/listener_manager_factory.h` defines factory interfaces for creating listener managers and connection handlers.\\n\\n**Active Listeners and Socket Sharing**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_listener.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveTcpListener` which wraps active TCP listeners and manages TCP connections. Multiple workers share sockets when bind_type is `NoReusePort`, with each worker getting the same socket from `ListenSocketFactoryImpl::getListenSocket(worker_index)`.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_socket.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveTcpSocket` which wraps accepted sockets going through listener filters.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_stream_listener_base.h` and `.cc` provide the base `ActiveStreamListenerBase` class and `OwnedActiveStreamListenerBase` mixin which owns active connections organized by filter chain in `ActiveConnections` containers.\\n- `source/server/active_listener_base.h` defines `ActiveListenerImplBase` base class for all active listeners with stats tracking.\\n- `source/server/active_udp_listener.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveUdpListenerBase` and `ActiveRawUdpListener` for UDP listeners.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/active_raw_udp_listener_config.h` and `.cc` implement `ActiveRawUdpListenerFactory`.\\n\\n**Drain Mechanism**:\\n- `source/server/drain_manager_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `DrainManagerImpl` which manages the listener drain sequence, controlling when connections should be drained during shutdown.\\n- The listener manager's `drainListener()` method transitions listeners from active to draining state and schedules drain completion via `DrainingFilterChainsManager::startDrainSequence()`.\\n- Filter chains can be selectively drained via `inPlaceFilterChainUpdate()` which calls `drainFilterChains()` for updated listeners.\\n\\n**Filter Chain Management**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `FilterChainManagerImpl` and `FilterChainImpl` for managing filter chains per listener.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_factory_context_callback.h` defines the `FilterChainFactoryContextCreator` interface.\\n\\n**Dynamic Listener Configuration**:\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/lds_api.h` and `.cc` implement `LdsApiImpl` which subscribes to LDS updates from the control plane.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h` implements `ProdListenerComponentFactory` which creates sockets via `ListenerComponentFactory::createListenSocket()` with bind_type parameter controlling socket sharing strategy.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure**:\\n- `source/server/listener_hooks.h` defines `ListenerHooks` interface for integration testing during listener lifecycle events.\\n- `source/common/listener_manager/listener_info_impl.h` and `.cc` implement `ListenerInfoImpl` for listener metadata.\\n- `source/common/quic/active_quic_listener.h` and `.cc` implement QUIC-specific listener handling.\\n- `source/extensions/bootstrap/internal_listener/` provides internal listener registry and management.\\n- `source/extensions/listener_managers/validation_listener_manager/` provides a validation listener manager factory for config validation.\\n- `source/common/network/listen_socket_impl.h` and `.cc` implement socket binding and option handling.\\n\\nThe architecture uses a thread-per-worker design where the listener manager on the main thread coordinates listener lifecycle changes across worker threads via the connection handler. Socket sharing between workers is implemented through socket duplication for no-reuse_port mode (managed by `ListenSocketFactoryImpl`) or per-worker socket creation for reuse_port mode. Drain state transitions are coordinated through the drain manager and tracked via listener states (active, warming, draining).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
